***juist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a> (419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">juust</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">juste</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">iūstus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*jowestos</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂yew-</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">just</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:juk.html>juk</a> (22523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">joc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">juc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:juk.html>juk</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*juką</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yugóm</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:joch.html>Joch</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:jok.html>jok</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">yoke</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">åg</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ok.html>ok</a></i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>a yoke</li>

***jukebox.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jukebox.html>jukebox</a> (17020)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1939, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">juke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roadside café</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">box</i>, replacing older <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nickel-in-a-slot phonograph</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jukebox.html>jukebox</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jukeboxes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A coin-operated machine that plays recorded music; it <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> push-buttons to make selections. <span class="defdate">[from 1939]</span>
<ul><li><b>1939</b>, <i>Life,</i> Dec 18, 1939, p. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=50EEAAAAMBAJamp;pg=PA27">27</a>:
<dl><dd>Glenn Miller plays more sweet numbers than hot. His greatest success <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> with the “<b>juke boxes</b>”, the nickel-in-a-slot automatic phonographs. Miller <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> easily the most outstanding juke-box artist of 1939.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An automated <a href = vnd.unilang:carousel.html>carousel</a> for the storage and retrieval of <a href = vnd.unilang:tapes.html>tapes</a>, CD-ROMs, etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A software application capable of replaying <a href = vnd.unilang:tracks.html>tracks</a> from a digital music collection.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b>,  Keith Underdahl,  <cite>Adobe Premiere Pro For <a href = vnd.unilang:dummies.html>Dummies</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Before you export a movie to tape, double-check the following: Make sure all unnecessary programs are closed, including your e-mail program, MP3 <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jukebox.html>jukebox</a></b>, and Web browser.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jukebox.html>jukebox</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">jukeboxes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jukeboxing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jukeboxed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To play and listen to music from a <a href = vnd.unilang:jukebox.html>jukebox</a>.

<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Sojourner,  <cite>Delicate: <a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>Stories</a></cite>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 238:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">She'd <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> forty-four, him forty-two when they <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a>, both of them drinking a little too much, both of them fed up with romance. <p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">jump</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">suit</i>, referring to <a href = vnd.unilang:parachute.html>parachute</a> jumps.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jumpsuit.html>jumpsuit</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jumpsuits.html>jumpsuits</a></b>)
</p>

***jute.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jute.html>jute</a> (51557)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bengali_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bengali language">Bengali</a></span> <i class="Beng mention" lang="bn">ঝুট</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jhuṭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">जूट</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jūṭa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twisted hair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jute.html>jute</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jutes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The coarse, strong fiber of the East Indian plants, <i>Corchorus olitorius</i> and <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Corchorus_capsularis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Corchorus capsularis"><i>Corchorus capsularis</i></a></span>, used to make <a href = vnd.unilang:mats.html>mats</a>, paper, <a href = vnd.unilang:gunny.html>gunny</a> cloth etc.</li>
<li>The plants from which this fibre <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> obtained.</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jood.html>jood</a></i>, with the connotation <i>to attempt to gain an unfair price in a business deal</i>. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used because the police fine people as a punishment.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kekǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kēkǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kakǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kaukǭ</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*keukǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jaw; palate; pharynx</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵyewh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to chew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Sooke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheek</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tsjeak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jaw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cheek</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">käke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jaw; jowl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">kjake</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jaw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kók</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mouth; gullet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaal.html>kaal</a> (5472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:cale.html>cale</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kalo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kalwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">naked, bald</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*galw-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">naked, bald</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kahl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">keal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">callow</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaal.html>kaal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaler.html>kaler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">kaalst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>without defining features, smooth, bland, plain</li>
<li>bald, bare, without fur, plumage, foliage etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a person<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> skinned, without means, in a poor state</li></ol>

***kaars.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaars.html>kaars</a> (7049)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kerse</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cāerse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">kerza</i>, from either <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cērāta</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">charta</i>. See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kerze</i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">câse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kāsi</i>, from late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*kāsī</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cāseus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***kaaskop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaaskop.html>kaaskop</a> (54174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaas.html>kaas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheese</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cup”, “head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaaskop.html>kaaskop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaaskoppen.html>kaaskoppen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaaskop.html>kaaskopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a mold in which Edam cheese <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> pressed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> idiot, stupid person</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Dutch person (in general)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Southern Netherlands</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Hollander</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>As a term for a Dutch person <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kaaskop.html>kaaskop</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also often used in a self-referential or self-deprecating manner. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not considered particularly insulting.
</p>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kopkaas</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kaaskop.html>kaaskop</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:scheldwoord.html>scheldwoord</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> Nederlander.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:daarentegen.html>daarentegen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> pukkelig <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blond.html>blond</a> vlashaar, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> onvervalste <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kaaskop.html>kaaskop</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a>.  <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kabelbaan.html>kabelbaan</a> (47142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kabel.html>kabel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baan.html>baan</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***kabeljauw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kabeljauw.html>kabeljauw</a> (23468)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cabelliau</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">cabillau</i>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">baculum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stick, staff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, referring to the way cod <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> split and dried on wooden <a href = vnd.unilang:sticks.html>sticks</a>.  Or, with metathesis from/influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Basque_language" class="extiw" title="w:Basque language">Basque</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="eu">bakailao</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kabeljauw.html>kabeljauw</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kabeljauwen.html>kabeljauwen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kabeljauw.html>kabeljauwtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A cod, fish of the family Gadidae.</li>
<li>Atlantic cod, <i>Gadus morhua</i>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kabeljauwfilet</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kabeljauwvisser</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bakkeljauw</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:kabeljauw.html>kabeljauw</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>vissen</a>)</span> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Gadus_morhua" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Gadus morhua"><span style="color:green;"><i>Gadus morhua</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, <a href = vnd.unilang:middelgrote.html>middelgrote</a> zoutwatervis, <a href = vnd.unilang:uitstekende.html>uitstekende</a> consumptievis, <a href = vnd.unilang:bedreigd.html>bedreigd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> overbevissing</li></ol>

***kabouter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kabouter.html>kabouter</a> (16088)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly already from Middle Dutch. Equivalent to a compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">koof</i> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kove</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kovo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kubô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a>, shed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) and a less certain second element that might be <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>hou</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">friendly, favorable disposition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kobold.html>Kobold</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kabouter.html>kabouter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kabouters.html>kabouters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kaboutertje.html>kaboutertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">fiction<span class="ib-comma">,</span> folklore</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A (now usually benevolent) tiny folkloric bearded <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> who traditionally wears a pointy red hat, <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a> in harmony with nature and resides in mushrooms or trees, similar to a gnome, <a href = vnd.unilang:leprechaun.html>leprechaun</a> or brownie.</li></ol>

***kachel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kachel.html>kachel</a> (11678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kacheloven</i>, partially a borrowing, partially a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kachelofen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kachel.html>Kachel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ofen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuiven.html>stove</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The original sense of “tiled stove” <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> generalized to any type of <a href = vnd.unilang:stuiven.html>stove</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kachel.html>kachel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kachels.html>kachels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kacheltje.html>kacheltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:stuiven.html>stove</a> (closed heating device)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoof.html>stoof</a></span></li></ul>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bargoens" class="extiw" title="w:Bargoens">Bargoens</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drunk</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
